Transit line A44E (ID: 196134_east) was a autobus line operating in 1961 in east Berlin with a service frequency of 10.0 minutes between vehicles and a vehicle capacity of 100 passengers. The line served 3 stations from Greifswalderstr. to S-Bhf. Mahlsdorf, including intermediate stops at Am Rosenhag. The line route passed through 1 neighborhoods: Mahlsdorf.
